# DOC-195 Redirect / 404 Audit: GitBook -> Mintlify Migration

_Generated audit of redirect coverage. Read-only analysis; no docs.json changes were made._

## Methodology

The legacy site was three separate GitBook spaces, each served at its own root:

| Legacy space         | Source dir            | New Mintlify prefix (per `migrate-to-mintlify.mjs`) |
| -------------------- | --------------------- | --------------------------------------------------- |
| Main docs (`guides`) | `docs/guides/`        | _(site root, no prefix)_                            |
| API reference        | `docs/api-reference/` | `/api`                                              |
| Brand guides         | `docs/brand-guides/`  | `/device-and-system-integration-guides`             |

**What I enumerated as legacy public URLs:**

1. The `redirects:` blocks in all three `.gitbook.yaml` files (existing public URLs that already had redirects and must continue to resolve): **130** entries (main: see `.gitbook.yaml`; brand: `docs/brand-guides/.gitbook.yaml`; api-reference has none).
2. The actual `.md` file tree under `docs/` (URL = path minus space root, `README.md` -> dir root, minus `.md`): **605** file-derived URLs.

**What I enumerated as existing/new routes:** 3. The `.mdx` file tree under `mintlify-docs/` (route = path minus `.mdx`, `index.mdx` -> dir root): **410** routes. 4. **API Reference endpoint pages are NOT `.mdx` files** — they are generated from `mintlify-docs/openapi.json` (referenced via `navigation.tabs[].openapi`). Each of the **196 OpenAPI operations carries an `x-mint.href`** (e.g. `/api/access_codes/create`) which is the page's route. I added all of these to the resolvable-route set. 5. The **42 existing `redirects` in `docs.json`** (all `/api/<resource>/index` -> `/api/<resource>/object` renames).

**Gap definition:** a legacy URL is a GAP when no Mintlify page exists at that path AND no existing `docs.json` redirect source matches it. For each gap the destination was chosen by: (a) the GitBook redirect's mapped target if it resolves; (b) the migration script's prefix mapping if the prefixed page exists; (c) unique slug match; (d) API resource index -> `/object` (mirroring the existing index->object pattern); (e) nearest existing ancestor.

### Counts

| Metric                                                                            | Count                            |
| --------------------------------------------------------------------------------- | -------------------------------- |
| Legacy public URLs enumerated (file-derived + gitbook-redirect sources, de-duped) | 605 files + 130 redirect sources |
| New Mintlify routes (`.mdx` + OpenAPI `x-mint.href` + existing redirects)         | 410 mdx + 196 api + 42 redirects |
| Already covered (page exists or existing redirect)                                | (all non-gap legacy URLs)        |
| **Gaps (need new redirect)**                                                      | **414**                          |
| High confidence                                                                   | 414                              |
| Medium confidence                                                                 | 0                                |
| Low confidence                                                                    | 0                                |
| Unresolved                                                                        | 0                                |

All 414 gaps resolved to high confidence (real destination pages verified to exist). No unresolved items.

#### Gap categories

- **API Reference resource index pages** (42): clean `/api/<resource>` legacy URLs (the GitBook `README.md` per resource) -> `/api/<resource>/object`. The existing docs.json redirects only cover the `/index` variant, not the clean path.
- **Guide relocations** (65): `quickstart/*`, `going-live`, `core-concepts/workspaces/*` -> `core-concepts/authentication/*`, `capability-guides/{smart-locks,access-systems}` -> `low-level-apis/*`, `capability-guides/access-grants` -> `use-cases/granting-access`, `products/*` -> `low-level-apis/*`.
- **Brand-guide path move** (307): legacy brand pages served at bare root slugs (e.g. `/avigilon-alta-access-system`) and `*-in-development` slugs -> `/device-and-system-integration-guides/<slug>`.

## UNRESOLVED — needs human decision

None. All 414 gaps were mapped to a verified existing destination page with high confidence.

### Review notes (confident, but worth a human glance)

- **Brand-guide bare-root slugs.** 246 of the brand redirects use **bare root-level legacy slugs** (e.g. `/akiles-locks`, `/avigilon-alta-access-system`). These are valid: the brand GitBook site served pages at its own root, and `docs/brand-guides/.gitbook.yaml` redirect sources confirm bare slugs were public URLs. They now redirect into `/device-and-system-integration-guides/<slug>`. Confirm none of these bare slugs are intended as live top-level Mintlify pages (none currently are).
- **`*-in-development` -> stable brand slugs.** Several legacy ASSA ABLOY Visionline / Vingcard "...-in-development" deep paths redirect to the now-stable `assa-abloy-visionline-access-control-system` / `assa-abloy-vingcard-credential-services` trees. Some deep credential-type subpages collapse to the section README (carried over verbatim from the GitBook redirect map).
- **`/api/<resource>` -> `/api/<resource>/object`.** Mirrors the existing `/api/<resource>/index -> /object` convention already in docs.json.
